[10/04/22, 4:58:42‚ÄØPM] ~‚ÄØAnjan Banerji: I am joining late in this discussion. My personal philosophy is to be a Trusted Advisor. A Trusted Advisor is one who practices values and systems which are transparent, fair and ‚ÄúFor client‚Äù recommendations. So far I have always stated and received my commission without any reservations. Like most of my respected associates here, the difference is not selling anything and everything but respecting the client‚Äôs mandate of location, and commercial budget being able to offer a choice of properties from the vast array of other options available in the market. The client saves time and effort and in my opinion that is worth more than the standard commission that we rightfully charge as our professional fees. 
My humble suggestion is to build this philosophy into well stated principles and conduct and give that a wide publicity. The other principles stated by others are no less important. I will be happy to offer my time to help people draft content for the use of our profession. 
Time to fight back with dignity and forthrightness.
